[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:460[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:400[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:324[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpander.jav[0m[1;92ma:204[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: a87e9aa6b0374484[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA critical security exception [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was raised by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer’s file path traversal sanitizer when the fuzzer fed specially crafted input [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto the `Expander.expand` methods in the Apache Commons Compress examples. The [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer detected a directory-escaping path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive extraction scenario, indicating a file path traversal vulnerability.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer input triggered a file path traversal detection within the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive-expansion logic. Instead of being confined to the intended extraction [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m[39m…[0m[35m/output/q/r/s/[0m[95mt[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the constructed path included [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“..[0m[35m/[0m[95m..[0m[39m” segments, allowing an archive entry to escape its target directory and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially overwrite arbitrary filesystem locations.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  File path traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39malso known as “directory traversal”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m – a security flaw that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menables an attacker to read, write or overwrite files outside the intended [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory by using relative path components.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations and Findings  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The security check is performed in [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcom.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmethods: `check`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`checkPath`, `pathFirstArgHook`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception occurs inside multiple overloads of `Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m in `Expander.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating a systemic lack of normalization[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor validation of archive entry names.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m merely invokes the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexample‐level API and is not itself vulnerable; it surfaces the underlying issue in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe example code.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `Expander` class in `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples` – examine[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall `[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` overloads for how archive entry names are processed and joined [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the output directory.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Name normalization and validation routines – look for missing calls to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`File#getCanonicalPath` or similar functions to resolve and verify target paths.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Interaction points with the Jazzer sanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FilePathTraversal`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m – [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand the expectations of the sanitizer and how the example code violates [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Any helper classes or utilities involved in path concatenation, filtering or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation of output directories, to confirm consistent application of [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory-escape protections.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m440[0m[39m:     * Expands [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@code archive[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m into [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@code targetDirectory[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:        try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:            return [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:            return outputFile;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.jav[0m[1;92ma:78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m89[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:    default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:        final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath, name, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:            return [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:            return outputFile;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability resides in the default `[0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation in `ArchiveEntry.java`.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It first resolves and normalizes the raw entry name, enforcing a bounds check,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut then blindly returns `[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without re‐normalizing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor re‐checking.   Consequently, decoded names containing “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” segments can escape [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe target directory.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Insight and Impacted Logic  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` overloads delegate to the generic [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mArchiveEntrySupplier, ArchiveEntryBiConsumer, Path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method, which invokes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fixing `resolveIn` at its source closes the traversal gap across every archive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformat [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZIP, TAR, 7z, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without touching `Expander` or fuzzing harness code.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Proposed Patch [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `ArchiveEntry.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Always decode the entry name first.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Resolve the decoded name against `parentPath`.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Normalize the resulting path.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Enforce that the normalized path begins with `parentPath`.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Return the normalized, validated path.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. If URL decoding fails, fall back to the raw name but still normalize and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Pseudo‐code change:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       String decodedName;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m[1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           decodedName = name;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       Path target = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, parentPath, name, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return target;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Step‐by‐Step Implementation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the existing `default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace its body with the above pseudo‐code logic:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Decode the entry name once.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Perform resolve + normalize + check on the decoded name.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Remove the old two‐stage resolve [0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw‐normalize + check, then raw‐resolve [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout check[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Recompile and run existing example tests to ensure no regressions.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preservation of Functionality  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Directory entries and flat names continue to be extracted as before.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Percent‐encoded names are decoded and treated as intended.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any path that would previously pass the first check but escape in the second [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mphase is now correctly rejected.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Addressing the Fuzzer Findings  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer‐triggered path “..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m” no longer bypasses [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization because decoding happens first and that path is immediately [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalized and flagged as outside `parentPath`.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer will no longer see a legitimate [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelative‐escape build, so `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` will not be raised for this[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvector.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Edge cases: Archives with unusual encoding [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnon‐ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m still fall back to the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraw name path, which is normalized and bounds‐checked.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to fuzzer harness or test suites; existing tests should pass.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Broad use of the same `resolveIn` upgrade ensures complete coverage across all[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marchive‐type overloads.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. References & Precedents  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach mirrors best practices in other Apache projects [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., tar‐slip [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmitigation in Commons VFS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures a single‐location fix in the shared `ArchiveEntry` interface rather [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthan scattered per‐format patches.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The fuzzer triggered a Jazzer security exception reporting a file path traversal    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         vulnerability when expanding archive entries via `Expander.expand`. To mitigate Zip [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         slip, a patch was proposed in `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`: the code now decodes the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entry name with `URLDecoder` before resolving and normalizing the path and then     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         checks for traversal. When applied, the modified `ArchiveEntry.java` failed to      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         compile under Maven, producing a single compilation error about the local variable  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `decodedName` possibly being assigned twice. The build aborted at that error.       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - During fuzzing with Jazzer, the code under test threw a                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` for “File path traversal,” indicating that a crafted  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         archive entry name allowed path traversal outside the intended extraction           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory.                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The stack trace shows the failure in `FilePathTraversal.check` called via         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`, originating in `Expander.expand` and          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ultimately in the fuzzer entry point `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - No application-level exception handling prevented the detection, and Jazzer’s     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sanitizer raised a critical security issue.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:            return outputFile;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/examples/Expander.jav[0m[1;92ma:67[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m75[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    private <T extends ArchiveEntry> void [0m[1;35mexpand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal ArchiveEntrySupplier<T> [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupplier, final ArchiveEntryBiConsumer<T> writer, final Path targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:            throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:        final boolean nullTarget = targetDirectory == null;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:        final Path targetDirPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:        T nextEntry = [0m[1;35msupplier.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:        while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry != null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:            final Path targetPath = nullTarget ? null : [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnextEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnextEntry.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!nullTarget && ![0m[1;35mFiles.isDirectory[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause & Symptoms  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The introduced `decodedName` logic in `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` triggered a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava definite‐assignment compilation error [0m[1;39m([0m[39m“variable decodedName might already [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhave been assigned”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The security problem [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZip-slip via percent-encoded paths[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unless we [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecode → normalize → check in a single, unambiguous control flow.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Critical Logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must decode the archive-entry name [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto catch percent-encoded “..” [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must normalize the resulting path and enforce the “[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m” [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck strictly **after** decoding.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter the fuzzer or harness code or impair existing archive-format[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msupport.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix Compilation & Security  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `ArchiveEntry.java`, revise the `resolveIn` method as follows:  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Declare a **non‐final** `decodedName` variable initialized to the raw [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`name`.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Attempt to URL‐decode it, overriding the variable only on successful [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecode; on exception, leave it as the raw name.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Resolve `decodedName` against `parentPath`, normalize that path, then [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforce the zip-slip check in one place.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Return the normalized, safety-checked `Path`.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. This eliminates the “might already have been assigned” error because there is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexactly one guaranteed initialization and, if decoding succeeds, one overwrite, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39motherwise none.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove any now-unused imports [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `UnsupportedEncodingException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesired.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the default `Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace its body with the following logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno other methods are touched[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Original entry name[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Decode percent-encodings, falling back to raw name on failure[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          String decodedName = name;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException ignore[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m keep decodedName == name[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Resolve & normalize decoded path[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path target = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Enforce parentPath prefix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mZip-slip mitigation[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, parentPath, name, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Safe, normalized path[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return target;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Update the imports at the top if desired:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure `import java.net.URLDecoder;` and `import [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjava.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;` remain.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Either keep or remove `import java.io.UnsupportedEncodingException;` based [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon whether you prefer catching it explicitly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno functional change[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By initializing `decodedName` and conditionally overwriting it, we satisfy [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava’s definite‐assignment rules and eliminate the compile error.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We continue to decode **before** normalization, catching any percent-encoded [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal attempts, then normalize and check exactly once.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing functionality—extracting archive entries in both unencoded and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencoded scenarios—remains intact, and no other code paths are altered.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We avoid any changes to the fuzzing harness, the fuzzer entry points, or test [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode, so test suites and fuzzers continue to operate as before.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side-Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change to archive formats beyond path handling—tests for Tar, Zip, AR, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39metc., still use the same method.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new code still tolerates invalid or malicious percent-encodings by falling[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mback to raw names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich are then checked[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing the `final` modifier on `decodedName` has no adverse effect outside [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis method.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If one prefers to remove the `UnsupportedEncodingException` import altogether,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39myou can safely eliminate it because `US_ASCII` is always supported in Java SE.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Additional File Retrieval Needed  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All context is within `ArchiveEntry.java`. No other parts of the repository [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequire changes to address this error or the root Zip-slip issue.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
